          Yorktown Crier-Poquoson Post\n             </a>\n            </i>\n            \xe2\x80\x93\n            <a href="/wiki/Yorktown,_Virginia" title="Yorktown, Virginia">\n             Yorktown\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n          <h3>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="Magazines">\n            Magazines\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n            <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hampton_Roads&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Magazines">\n             edit\n            </a>\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             ]\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </h3>\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Coastal Virginia Magazine\n           </i>\n           is one of the region\'s city and lifestyle magazine. The publication is published eight times a year and covers all of Hampton Roads and the\n           <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Shore_of_Virginia" title="Eastern Shore of Virginia">\n            Eastern Shore of Virginia\n           </a>\n           .\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Coastal_Virginia_Magazine_104-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Coastal_Virginia_Magazine-104">\n             [104]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           <i>\n            Coastal Virginia Magazine\n           </i>\n           was formerly known as\n           <i>\n            Hampton Roads Magazine\n           </i>\n           .\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Hampton Roads Times\n           </i>\n           serves as an online magazine for the region.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Suffolk Living Magazine\n           </i>\n           is another of the region\'s city and lifestyle magazines. The publication is published four times a year and covers the City of Suffolk. Suffolk Publications also produces Virginia-Carolina Boomers, a regional guide for Boomers in the area, which comes out twice a year.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Suffolk_Living_Magazine_105-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Suffolk_Living_Magazine-105">\n             [105]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </p>\n          <h3>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="Television">\n            Television\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n            <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hampton_Roads&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Television">\n             edit\n            </a>\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             ]\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </h3>\n          <p>\n           The Hampton Roads\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Designated_market_area" title="Designated market area">\n            designated market area\n           </a>\n           (DMA) is the 42nd largest in the U.S. with 712,790 homes (0.64% of the total U.S.).\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nielsen_106-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-nielsen-106">\n             [106]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           The major network television affiliates are\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WTKR-TV" title="WTKR-TV">\n            WTKR-TV\n           </a>\n           3 (\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Columbia_Broadcasting_Service" title="Columbia Broadcasting Service">\n            CBS\n           </a>\n           ),\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WAVY" title="WAVY">\n            WAVY\n           </a>\n           10 (\n           <a href="/wiki/NBC" title="NBC">\n            NBC\n           </a>\n           ),\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WVEC-TV" title="WVEC-TV">\n            WVEC-TV\n           </a>\n           13 (\n           <a href="/wiki/American_Broadcasting_Company" title="American Broadcasting Company">\n            ABC\n           </a>\n           ),\n           <a href="/wiki/WGNT" title="WGNT">\n            WGNT\n           </a>\n           27 (\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/The_CW_Television_Network" title="The CW Television Network">\n            CW\n           </a>\n           ),\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WTVZ" title="WTVZ">\n            WTVZ\n           </a>\n           33 (\n           <a href="/wiki/MyNetworkTV" title="MyNetworkTV">\n            MyNetworkTV\n           </a>\n           ),\n           <a href="/wiki/WVBT" title="WVBT">\n            WVBT\n           </a>\n           43 (\n           <a href="/wiki/Fox_Broadcasting_Company" title="Fox Broadcasting Company">\n            Fox\n           </a>\n           ), and\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WPXV" title="WPXV">\n            WPXV\n           </a>\n           49 (\n           <a href="/wiki/Ion_Television" title="Ion Television">\n            Ion Television\n           </a>\n           ). The\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Public_Broadcasting_Service" title="Public Broadcasting Service">\n            Public Broadcasting Service\n           </a>\n           station is\n           <a href="/wiki/WHRO-TV" title="WHRO-TV">\n            WHRO-TV\n           </a>\n           15.\n           <a href="/wiki/UNC-TV" title="UNC-TV">\n            WUND 2\n           </a>\n           (\n           <a href="/wiki/UNC-TV" title="UNC-TV">\n            UNC-TV\n           </a>\n           /\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Public_Broadcasting_Service" title="Public Broadcasting Service">\n            PBS member station\n           </a>\n           ), broadcasting out of\n           <a href="/wiki/Edenton,_North_Carolina" title="Edenton, North Carolina">\n            Edenton, North Carolina\n           </a>\n           , serves as another PBS affiliate for the area. Area residents also can receive independent stations, such as\n           <a href="/wiki/WSKY-TV" title="WSKY-TV">\n            WSKY\n           </a>\n           broadcasting on channel 4 from the Outer Banks of North Carolina,\n           <a href="/wiki/WGBS-LD" title="WGBS-LD">\n            WGBS-LD\n           </a>\n           broadcasting on channel 11 from Hampton, and\n           <a href="/wiki/WTPC-TV" title="WTPC-TV">\n            WTPC 21\n           </a>\n           , a\n           <a href="/wiki/Trinity_Broadcasting_Network" title="Trinity Broadcasting Network">\n            TBN\n           </a>\n           affiliate out of Virginia Beach. Most Hampton Roads localities are served by\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cox_Cable" title="Cox Cable">\n            Cox Cable\n           </a>\n           which provides\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LNC_5" title="LNC 5">\n            LNC 5\n           </a>\n           , a local\n           <a href="/wiki/24-hour_news_cycle" title="24-hour news cycle">\n            24-hour\n           </a>\n           <a href="/wiki/United_States_cable_news" title="United States cable news">\n            cable news\n           </a>\n           television network. Suffolk, Franklin, Isle of Wight, and Southampton are served by Charter Communications.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n            <a href="#cite_note-107">\n             [107]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Verizon_FiOS" title="Verizon FiOS">\n            Verizon FiOS\n           </a>\n           service is currently available in parts of the region and continues to expand, offering a non-satellite alternative to Cox.\n           <a href="/wiki/DirecTV" title="DirecTV">\n            DirecTV\n           </a>\n           and\n           <a href="/wiki/Dish_Network" title="Dish Network">\n            Dish Network\n           </a>\n           are also popular as an alternative to cable television.\n          </p>\n          <h3>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="Radio">\n            Radio\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n            <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hampton_Roads&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Radio">\n             edit\n            </a>\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             ]\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </h3>\n          <p>\n           Norfolk is served by a variety of radio stations on the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Template:Hampton_Roads_FM" title="Template:Hampton Roads FM">\n            FM\n           </a>\n           and\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Template:Hampton_Roads_AM" title="Template:Hampton Roads AM">\n            AM\n           </a>\n           dials, with towers located around the Hampton Roads area. These cater to many different interests, including news,\n           <a href="/wiki/Talk_radio" title="Talk radio">\n            talk radio\n           </a>\n           , and sports, as well as an eclectic mix of musical interests.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hampton_Roads_Radio_Links_108-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Hampton_Roads_Radio_Links-108">\n             [108]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </p>\n          <h2>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">\n            Sports\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n            <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hampton_Roads&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Sports">\n             edit\n            </a>\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             ]\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </h2>\n          <h3>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="Team_sports">\n            Team sports\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n            <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hampton_Roads&amp;action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: Team sports">\n             edit\n            </a>\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             ]\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </h3>\n          <p>\n           Norfolk serves as home to two professional franchises, the\n           <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Tides" title="Norfolk Tides">\n            Norfolk Tides\n           </a>\n           of the\n           <a href="/wiki/International_League" title="International League">\n            International League\n           </a>\n           and the\n           <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Admirals_(ECHL)" title="Norfolk Admirals (ECHL)">\n            Norfolk Admirals\n           </a>\n           of the\n           <a href="/wiki/ECHL" title="ECHL">\n            ECHL\n           </a>\n           .\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tides_109-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Tides-109">\n             [109]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           The Tides play at\n           <a href="/wiki/Harbor_Park" title="Harbor Park">\n            Harbor Park\n           </a>\n           , seating 12,067 and opened in 1993. The Admirals play at\n           <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Scope" title="Norfolk Scope">\n            Norfolk Scope\n           </a>\n           Arena, seating 8,725 or 13,800 festival seating, which opened in 1971. Hampton Roads was formerly home to the\n           <a href="/wiki/American_Basketball_Association" title="American Basketball Association">\n            ABA\n           </a>\n           <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Squires" title="Virginia Squires">\n            Virginia Squires\n           </a>\n           , alternating between Norfolk and Hampton, as well as Richmond and Roanoke. The Squires folded in 1976, after the league merged with the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NBA" title="NBA">\n            NBA\n           </a>\n           .\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           The\n           <a href="/wiki/Peninsula_Pilots" title="Peninsula Pilots">\n            Peninsula Pilots\n           </a>\n           play in the\n           <a href="/wiki/Coastal_Plain_League" title="Coastal Plain League">\n            Coastal Plain League\n           </a>\n           , a summer baseball league. The Pilots play in Hampton at\n           <a href="/wiki/War_Memorial_Stadium_(Hampton)" title="War Memorial Stadium (Hampton)">\n            War Memorial Stadium\n           </a>\n           seating 5,125 and opened in 1948.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Peninsula_Pilots_110-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Peninsula_Pilots-110">\n             [110]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           On the collegiate level, four\n           <a href="/wiki/NCAA_Division_I" title="NCAA Division I">\n            Division I\n           </a>\n           programs\xe2\x80\x94two on the Southside and two on the Peninsula\xe2\x80\x94field teams in many sports, including football, basketball, and baseball; three currently play football in the second-tier\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Football_Championship_Subdivision" title="Football Championship Subdivision">\n            FCS\n           </a>\n           , while ODU recently moved up to the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NCAA_Division_I-A" title="NCAA Division I-A">\n            FBS\n           </a>\n           football. The Southside boasts the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Old_Dominion_Monarchs" title="Old Dominion Monarchs">\n            Old Dominion Monarchs\n           </a>\n           and the\n           <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_State_Spartans" title="Norfolk State Spartans">\n            Norfolk State Spartans\n           </a>\n           , both in Norfolk, while the Peninsula features the\n           <a href="/wiki/William_%26_Mary_Tribe" title="William &amp; Mary Tribe">\n            William &amp; Mary Tribe\n           </a>\n           in Williamsburg and\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hampton_Pirates" title="Hampton Pirates">\n            Hampton Pirates\n           </a>\n           in Hampton. W&amp;M is a member of the\n           <a href="/wiki/Colonial_Athletic_Association" title="Colonial Athletic Association">\n            Colonial Athletic Association\n           </a>\n           . Norfolk State and Hampton, both\n           <a href="/wiki/Historically_black_colleges_and_universities" title="Historically black colleges and universities">\n            historically black institutions\n           </a>\n           , compete in the\n           <a href="/wiki/Mid-Eastern_Athletic_Conference" title="Mid-Eastern Athletic Conference">\n            Mid-Eastern Athletic Conference\n           </a>\n           .\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Monarchs_111-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Monarchs-111">\n             [111]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Spartans_112-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Spartans-112">\n             [112]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tribe_113-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Tribe-113">\n             [113]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Pirates_114-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Pirates-114">\n             [114]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           ODU joined\n           <a href="/wiki/Conference_USA" title="Conference USA">\n            Conference USA\n           </a>\n           , an FBS football conference, as a full FBS member in 2015. The area also has two\n           <a href="/wiki/NCAA_Division_III" title="NCAA Division III">\n            Division III\n           </a>\n           programs, one in each subregion\xe2\x80\x94the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Virginia_Wesleyan_College" title="Virginia Wesleyan College">\n            Virginia Wesleyan Marlins\n           </a>\n           on the border of Virginia Beach and Norfolk,\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Marlins_115-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Marlins-115">\n             [115]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           and the\n           <a href="/wiki/Christopher_Newport_University#Athletics" title="Christopher Newport University">\n            Christopher Newport University Captains\n           </a>\n           in Newport News. The Captains sponsor fourteen sports and currently compete in the\n           <a href="/wiki/USA_South_Athletic_Conference" title="USA South Athletic Conference">\n            USA South Athletic Conference\n           </a>\n           ,\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n            <a href="#cite_note-116">\n             [116]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           but will move to the\n           <a href="/wiki/Capital_Athletic_Conference" title="Capital Athletic Conference">\n            Capital Athletic Conference\n           </a>\n           in July 2013.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           Virginia Beach serves as home to two soccer teams, the\n           <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads_Piranhas" title="Hampton Roads Piranhas">\n            Hampton Roads Piranhas\n           </a>\n           , a men\'s team in the\n           <a href="/wiki/Premier_Development_League" title="Premier Development League">\n            Premier Development League\n           </a>\n           , and a women\'s team by the same name in the\n           <a href="/wiki/USL_W-League" title="USL W-League">\n            W-League\n           </a>\n           . The Piranhas play at the\n           <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach_Sportsplex" title="Virginia Beach Sportsplex">\n            Virginia Beach Sportsplex\n           </a>\n           . The\n           <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach_Sportsplex" title="Virginia Beach Sportsplex">\n            Virginia Beach Sportsplex\n           </a>\n           , seating 11,541 and opened in 1999, contains the central training site for the U.S. women\'s national\n           <a href="/wiki/Field_hockey" title="Field hockey">\n            field hockey\n           </a>\n           team.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">\n            <a href="#cite_note-117">\n             [117]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           The Sportsplex was expanded to accommodate the\n           <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Destroyers" title="Virginia Destroyers">\n            Virginia Destroyers\n           </a>\n           , a franchise in the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_Football_League_(2009)" title="United Football League (2009)">\n            United Football League\n           </a>\n           which relocated from\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Florida_Tuskers" title="Florida Tuskers">\n            Orlando\n           </a>\n           . The Destroyers played in Virginia Beach from 2011-12, and won the 2011 league championship. The\n           <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=North_American_Sand_Soccer_Championships&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="North American Sand Soccer Championships (page does not exist)">\n            North American Sand Soccer Championships\n           </a>\n           , a\n           <a href="/wiki/Beach_soccer" title="Beach soccer">\n            beach soccer\n           </a>\n           tournament, is held annually on the beach in Virginia Beach.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           The\n           <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Nighthawks" title="Norfolk Nighthawks">\n            Norfolk Nighthawks\n           </a>\n           were a charter member of the\n           <a href="/wiki/Arena_Football_League" title="Arena Football League">\n            Arena Football League\n           </a>\n           \'s minor league,\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Af2" title="Af2">\n            af2\n           </a>\n           . They ceased operations in 2003 after their fourth season. Also, the\n           <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach_Mariners" title="Virginia Beach Mariners">\n            Virginia Beach Mariners\n           </a>\n           of soccer\'s\n           <a href="/wiki/USL_First_Division" title="USL First Division">\n            USL First Division\n           </a>\n           were active from 1994 until 2006.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           Hampton Roads is 130 miles (210\xc2\xa0km) from the nearest major sports teams in Washington, D.C. and\n           <a href="/wiki/Raleigh,_North_Carolina" title="Raleigh, North Carolina">\n            Raleigh, North Carolina\n           </a>\n           . Another significant issue with the area as a sports market is internal transportation. The metropolitan area is split into two\n           <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Peninsula" title="Virginia Peninsula">\n            distinct\n           </a>\n           <a href="/wiki/South_Hampton_Roads" title="South Hampton Roads">\n            parts\n           </a>\n           by its eponymous harbor; as of 2012, the harbor has only three widely separated road crossings (the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads_Bridge-Tunnel" title="Hampton Roads Bridge-Tunnel">\n            Hampton Roads Bridge-Tunnel\n           </a>\n           ,\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Monitor-Merrimac_Memorial_Bridge-Tunnel" title="Monitor-Merrimac Memorial Bridge-Tunnel">\n            Monitor-Merrimac Memorial Bridge-Tunnel\n           </a>\n           , and\n           <a href="/wiki/James_River_Bridge" title="James River Bridge">\n            James River Bridge\n           </a>\n           ), each with two lanes of traffic in each direction. In addition, the area has two other major tunnels, plus several drawbridges on key highway corridors.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           Hampton Roads previously hosted a\n           <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Squires" title="Virginia Squires">\n            successful franchise\n           </a>\n           in the\n           <a href="/wiki/American_Basketball_Association" title="American Basketball Association">\n            American Basketball Association\n           </a>\n           , although it was never a full-time home for that team. Its highest-ranking teams as of 2015 are the\n           <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Admirals_(ECHL)" title="Norfolk Admirals (ECHL)">\n            Norfolk Admirals\n           </a>\n           of the\n           <a href="/wiki/ECHL" title="ECHL">\n            ECHL\n           </a>\n           , and the\n           <a href="/wiki/Norfolk_Tides" title="Norfolk Tides">\n            Norfolk Tides\n           </a>\n           of the\n           <a href="/wiki/International_League" title="International League">\n            IL\n           </a>\n           . Virginia is also the most populous state without a major team playing within its borders, though its northern reaches are served by the Washington clubs\xe2\x80\x94two of which, the NHL\'s\n           <a href="/wiki/Washington_Capitals" title="Washington Capitals">\n            Capitals\n           </a>\n           and NFL\'s\n           <a href="/wiki/Washington_Redskins" title="Washington Redskins">\n            Redskins\n           </a>\n           , have their operational headquarters and practice facilities in Virginia. Redskins owner\n           <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Snyder" title="Daniel Snyder">\n            Daniel Snyder\n           </a>\n           , through\n           <a href="/wiki/Red_Zebra_Broadcasting" title="Red Zebra Broadcasting">\n            a separate company\n           </a>\n           , owns two radio stations,\n           <a href="/wiki/WXTG_(AM)" title="WXTG (AM)">\n            WXTG\n           </a>\n           and\n           <a href="/wiki/WXTG-FM" title="WXTG-FM">\n            WXTG-FM\n           </a>\n           , in the Norfolk market. The Hampton Roads television market is ranked\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_TV_markets_and_major_sports_teams_in_the_United_States" title="List of TV markets and major sports teams in the United States">\n            42nd\n           </a>\n           in the U.S.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           There have been several failed projects to attract major league teams to Hampton Roads:\n          </p>\n          <ul>\n           <li>\n            In 1997, Norfolk presented a proposal to bring an expansion hockey team to Hampton Roads, but that initiative failed. The team was going to be called the\n            <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Roads_Rhinos" title="Hampton Roads Rhinos">\n             Hampton Roads Rhinos\n            </a>\n            .\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            In 2002, Norfolk presented a proposal to bring the Charlotte Hornets basketball team to southeastern Virginia, but New Orleans won the bid for the team, renaming it the\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Orleans_Hornets" title="New Orleans Hornets">\n             New Orleans Hornets\n            </a>\n            .\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            In 2004, Norfolk presented a proposal to bring the\n            <a href="/wiki/Montreal_Expos" title="Montreal Expos">\n             Montreal Expos\n            </a>\n            baseball team to the metro area, but Washington, D.C. won the bid for the team, renaming it the\n            <a href="/wiki/Washington_Nationals" title="Washington Nationals">\n             Washington Nationals\n            </a>\n            .\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            In 2012, there were talks of the Sacramento Kings of the NBA moving to a\n            <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach_Arena" title="Virginia Beach Arena">\n             proposed new arena\n            </a>\n            in Virginia Beach near the Oceanfront.\n            <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n             <a href="#cite_note-118">\n              [118]\n             </a>\n            </sup>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n          <h3>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="Individual_sports">\n            Individual sports\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n            <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hampton_Roads&amp;action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Individual sports">\n             edit\n            </a>\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             ]\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </h3>\n          <p>\n           The\n           <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Coliseum" title="Hampton Coliseum">\n            Hampton Coliseum\n           </a>\n           , seating 10,761 to 13,800 festival seating, hosts the annual\n           <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Virginia_Duals&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Virginia Duals (page does not exist)">\n            Virginia Duals\n           </a>\n           wrestling events, and the annual\n           <a href="/wiki/Hampton_Jazz_Festival" title="Hampton Jazz Festival">\n            Hampton Jazz Festival\n           </a>\n           . The arena opened in 1970 and has previously hosted\n           <a href="/wiki/Hampton_University" title="Hampton University">\n            Hampton University\n           </a>\n           basketball along with\n           <a href="/wiki/National_Basketball_Association" title="National Basketball Association">\n            NBA\n           </a>\n           and\n           <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">\n            NHL\n           </a>\n           preseason exhibition games.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           Virginia Beach is home to the\n           <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_Surfing_Championships" title="East Coast Surfing Championships">\n            East Coast Surfing Championships\n           </a>\n           , an annual contest of more than 100 of the world\'s top professional surfers and an estimated 400 amateur surfers. This is North America\'s oldest surfing contest, and features combined cash prizes of $40,000.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">\n            <a href="#cite_note-119">\n             [119]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           <a href="/wiki/Langley_Speedway_(Virginia)" title="Langley Speedway (Virginia)">\n            Langley Speedway\n           </a>\n           in Hampton, seating 6,500, hosts stock car races every weekend during spring, summer, and early fall.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Langley_Speedway_120-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-Langley_Speedway-120">\n             [120]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           The\n           <a href="/wiki/Kingsmill_Championship" title="Kingsmill Championship">\n            Kingsmill Championship\n           </a>\n           , an event on the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/LPGA_Tour" title="LPGA Tour">\n            LPGA Tour\n           </a>\n           , is contested annually on\n           <a href="/wiki/Mother%27s_Day" title="Mother\'s Day">\n            Mother\'s Day\n           </a>\n           weekend at Kingsmill Resort near Williamsburg.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           In 1998, 2001, 2006, and 2010 Hampton Roads was hosting the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/AAU_Junior_Olympics" title="AAU Junior Olympics">\n            AAU Junior Olympics\n           </a>\n           .\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-121">\n            <a href="#cite_note-121">\n             [121]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </p>\n          <h3>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="Professional_wrestling">\n            Professional wrestling\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n            <a href="/w/index.php?title=Hampton_Roads&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Professional wrestling">\n             edit\n            </a>\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             ]\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </h3>\n          <p>\n           Hampton Roads has hosted many professional wrestling events throughout the years. The Norfolk Scope has served as the site of these events, including\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Total_Nonstop_Action_Wrestling" title="Total Nonstop Action Wrestling">\n            Total Nonstop Action Wrestling\n           </a>\n           \'s\n           <a href="/wiki/Destination_X" title="Destination X">\n            Destination X\n           </a>\n           ,\n           <a href="/wiki/World_Championship_Wrestling" title="World Championship Wrestling">\n            World Championship Wrestling\n           </a>\n           \'s\n           <a href="/wiki/Starrcade" title="Starrcade">\n            Starrcade\n           </a>\n           and\n           <a href="/wiki/WCW_World_War_3" title="WCW World War 3">\n            World War 3\n           </a>\n           , and\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Wrestling_Entertainment" title="World Wrestling Entertainment">\n            WWF/WWE\'s\n           </a>\n           <a href="/wiki/The_Great_American_Bash" title="The Great American Bash">\n            The Great American Bash\n           </a>\n           and the 2011\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Slammy_Awards" title="Slammy Awards">\n            Slammy Awards\n           </a>\n           .\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122">\n            <a href="#cite_note-122">\n             [122]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           Norfolk Scope was also the site of an infamous episode of\n           <a href="/wiki/WCW_Monday_Nitro" title="WCW Monday Nitro">\n            WCW Monday Nitro\n           </a>\n           , where several members of the\n           <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Wrestling_Entertainment" title="World Wrestling Entertainment">\n            World Wrestling Federation\n           </a>\n           stable\n           <a href="/wiki/D-Generation_X" title="D-Generation X">\n            D-Generation X\n           </a>\n           literally drove a tank to the entryway of the Scope, thus "invading" the competition. The Hampton Coliseum has also hosted many events, including\n           <i>\n            <a href="/wiki/WWE_Raw" title="WWE Raw">\n             RAW\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           , in April 1998, August 2005, May 2007, January 2008, and July 2011, as well as\n           <i>\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WWE_Friday_Night_SmackDown" title="WWE Friday Night SmackDown">\n             SmackDown!\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           and for\n           <i>\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ECW_on_Sci_Fi" title="ECW on Sci Fi">\n             ECW on Sci Fi\n            </a>\n           </i>\n           on December 2006. In January 2008, WWE broadcast its first television show taped in\n           <a href="/wiki/High-definition_video" title="High-definition video">\n            high definition\n           </a>\n           from Hampton, Virginia.\n          </p>\n          <p>\n           The Hampton Roads area is also home to at least one professional wrestling promotion,\n           <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Vanguard_Championship_Wrestling&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Vanguard Championship Wrestling (page does not exist)">\n            Vanguard Championship Wrestling\n           </a>\n           , which holds events throughout the region, and has a weekly television show on the local Fox affiliate.\n          </p>\n          <h2>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n            See also\n           </span>\n           <span class="mw-editsection">\n            <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n             [\n            </span>\n Colonial Williamsburg\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Former_counties,_cities,_and_towns_of_Virginia" title="Former counties, cities, and towns of Virginia">\n             Former counties, cities, and towns of Virginia\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            <a href="/wiki/Historic_Triangle"    Jamestown, Virginia\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_people_from_Hampton_Roads" title="List of people from Hampton Roads">\n             List of people from Hampton Roads\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            <a href="/wiki/List_of_tallest_buildings_in_Norfolk,_Virginia" title="List of tallest buildings in Norfolk, Virginia">\n             List of tallest buildings in Norfolk, Virginia\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            <a Virginia Peninsula\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li>\n            <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Port_Authority" title="Virginia Port Authority">\n             Virginia Port Authority\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n          <h2>\n           <span class="mw-headline" id="References">\n            References\n           </span>\n           <span
